< Name>
Collin St.Dic< /Name>
<Resp>None<//Resp>< text>
I want to start off by saying the hostess, our wonderful server, and the food was absolutely impeccable! So, why the TWO STARS? Strictly for one reason... the owner. My partner and I, who just so happened to be the only POC in the establishment, were discriminated against.

Our night started off beautiful. The service was astounding and we even had some amazing conversations with other guests around us.

As the place evolved with more people, I began to notice the owner, a white, tall, assertive male would make rounds to each and every table, checking in on them. I was impressed by this level of detail and comforted to see how personable he was with his customers. I was eager to tell him it was my first time here, and being apart of the NoHo community, it was a little gem I discovered and couldn't wait to come back.

Unfortunately, that opportunity never happened. Why? Because for whatever reason, the owner decided to outright skip our table every time he made his rounds. I gave him the benefit of the doubt that maybe he was busy, or maybe he even were friends with some of the guests he was so conversational with. I watched him, each and every time ask every table around them how they were doing. He literally looked at me and my partner, (again the only POC in the entire restaurant at the time (Black and Hispanic)) and would again present pleasantries to the tables around us every time disregarding our presence... every... time. I said this has got to be a mistake or a joke.

My partner and I pointed out to the waitress this inconceivable and perceivable discrimination that was happening to us by the owner. Our waitress, who was more than understanding and was shocked we felt that way, reached out to the owner about our distaste of what we thought was clear discrimination. The owner then walked over to our table... Great, he's going to acknowledge how he made us feel uncomfortable and give us a small apology. Honestly, I would've been content with that. No, instead he gave us our check and said, "your beers were paid for by Table 9". Gave us our bill then simply walked away.

No acknowledgment. No apology. Nothing. Needless to say, I was appalled and shocked that during this racially tense climate, he would choose to not even acknowledge how uncomfortable we felt based off his actions in his own establishment.

It's shame because every other aspect of our experience was impeccable and he unfortunately put a stain on our night out, and I would advise any POC to be aware if you're going visit this restaurant.</text>

< text>
Walked in on Thursday evening and as you come in it's such a warm, surprisingly relaxing vibe!  it's so pretty! decided to sit at the beautiful carrara marble bar because, one, it was so pretty with all of the candles, and two, we wanted to visit with the bartenders and other wine drinkers and visit. We had a cheese and charcuterie board which was delicious, along with some really good herbed olives and some of the best bread I've ever had.  Started with a pilsner that was delicious and then shamelessly switched to wine including this really good Lambrusco on tap.  Then tasted a few other really good wines.  One plus is that we were able to order half glasses, so could taste a lot of different wines.  Even though we were soooo full, had to order the dessert which was berries with this decadent  heavy whipped Mascarpone (I think that's what it was).  it was goooood!    we had such a nice time here.  Highly recommend.<//text>

< text>
This is my first Google review, but with such a positive experience, I had to write this review. The first thing that comes to mind is the clean, courteous, and top notch grade-A professional service. As soon as I stepped through the front door, I wanted to do a double take on the name on the door. This is because I saw all the cozy amenities and thought I was walking into the front desk of a fancy health spa, rather than at a dental office.

I know a lot of people (even myself), have some kind of phobia/paranoia about visiting the dentist. This is usually from some childhood trauma, creepy movie horror stories, or just bad dental service. Trinity Family Dental is far from that. I actually left with a smile vs the typical dentist visit with a sore/numb mouth, a bewildered what the 'ef just happened to me attitude, and an empty wallet, or crazy payments. Thank-you Dr. Shen and all of the staff. You got a patient for life who plans to refer anyone and everyone I know to come here.< /text>

<username>d o< /username>< Review>
I am so happy I found Trinity Family Dentistry!  I had the same dentist for over 17 years and needed to find a new dentist.  I have anxiety getting dental work done, but Dr. Shen and his staff are amazing!

When you walk into their office you feel welcomed.  The front desk provided details about what insurance covered and what my out of pocket costs were. Prices were very affordable.

I had to get a root canal done on a crowned tooth.  Dr. Leah O'Campo, Dr. Shen, and Lauren did an amazing job.  I felt at ease with their light touch and felt no pain at all. I didn't feel anxious and was very comfortable.  They explained every step of the process.  All of their equipment is high tech.  I was able to get my crown done in less than 2 hours.  With Cerec there is no need to go through the messy and uncomfortable impression.  I didn't have to wait 2 weeks to come back to have the permanent crown placed.

I also had x-rays and my teeth thoroughly cleaned.  Summer took the time to tell me how I could keep my teeth and gums healthy without making me feel bad.

I am so thankful to have found Trinity Family Dentistry. They truly take the time to care for you health and are honest.</Review>

< Review>
I reached out to Dr. Shen because he is knowledgeable with military, veteran, and reserve. As a veteran, Dr. Shen understands the needs of service members and his staff are knowledgeable with Tricare and United Concordia Insurance. I drove 87 miles for my appointment. The staff accommodated me by making sure my paperwork was completed ahead of time. When I got to the office, I gave Dr. Shen my dental records and the night guard I had been using. He took the records and studied them while an assistant ushered me to the exam room for a full set of x-rays. When we were done, Dr. Shen asked me what I expected from the visit, and we proceeded to form the goals for the visit. With the aid of an assistant, he conducted a comprehensive exam. He presented his diagnosis and treatment plan based on my dental history, x-rays, and information gained from the examination. He then worked with his office to figure out how much my insurance would cover. He came back shortly with a very good price for services. The price was so good that I ended getting everything repaired in one visit. Six of my silver fillings were replaced with resin composite, a worn-out tooth was covered with a crown, and I was fitted for a new night guard. Everything took 3  1/2 hours. I probably would have left sooner, if Dr. Shen wasn't such a nice guy to talk to. I credit the whole office for the professional service and environment. But, I believe Dr. Shen deserves credit for his servant leadership. He showed up to the office at the same time, if not earlier than his staff. He treated his staff as equals and listened to their input. In turn, his team sought to educate me with their procedures, equipment, and dental health. They were attentive to my needs especially when I needed more anesthesia for pain. The whole experience made me feel like things were done right, for the right reasons.</Review>

We decided to try this place out since they had a family meal deal. $25 for 4 burgers and 2 orders of fries. My family is big, so we ordered chicken strips for the little ones. I must say... this place is a hidden gem for sure! The burger was amazing and the meat was seasoned nicely.  Fries were on the softer side. But we actually prefer fries like that. My prizes were a free beer on my next visit, which I'm sure will be another memorable experience. Great location next to the old Vogue theatre, featuring  a variety of outdoor seating. Family friendly.  There's clearly a reason this place stays busy, and I look forward to my next visit.

Highly recommended.<//review><Date>1614588782010< /Date>< Pics>

<date>1551864337072<//date><pictures>None<//pictures>< Review>
Decent store, albeit smaller than the other Ralphs' I've been to. But it's my local supermarket and it's convenient. Despite its smaller size it still has everything I need--size isn't everything, ha. :) Seriously though, there's no pharmacy, the deli is sort of small, and the other non grocery stuff you find at other supermarkets (including the other Ralph'ss like 2 mi away) probably isn't here.

It's organized, but sometimes seems a little dingy and I don't think there's a lot of care put into maintaining the shelves and deli area. It's a little expensive but there are some great deals with a club card membership thing.  The liquor aisle is always well stocked and kept clean, haha.

Employees...some of them are absolutely amazing and could easily work at a top tier exclusive hotel or something of that ilk. They go out of their way to help and always have time to chat. They're efficient, kind, helpful and generous. This is why I'm not giving it the 3 stars it would deserve should employees be taken out of the equation. There are other employees who do the bare minimum, of course. It's like a 5050 split.

Final score is 3.4</Review>

<user>117851340743297018984< /user><username>Jack Bouley</username>< time>
1551050827114< /time>
<Rating>5<//Rating>< Review>
This place is great. I'm new to City Heights from a small town in New Hampshire, and this place feels like home. All types of people shop here, but it's primarily a Mexican food store. It has lots of staple supplies, veggies, and the great darned chorizo I've ever had. The checkout staff is so nice, and the giant security guard at the front has a heart of gold. Even though everyone here is bilingual, I've even learned a little Spanish so I can impress these people. They learned English, so I should learn Spanish! The Mexican pastries and snacks are a little weird, but I love trying new things. This is a great neighborhood store, and I'm lucky to live right next door :)< /Review>

< Review>
This is my all-time favorite Mexican restaurant, because it's family owned and they GENUINELY care about their customers. We've loved this place for years.

My family and I just had the greatest meal from here. Got my favorite nachos with plenty of really juicy, tender chicken. My sister loved her chicken quesadilla which comes with PLENTY of chicken and cheese. My bro-in-law had a burrito filled with chunks of beef that just melt in your mouth -- wow. We always get the flan here, too, because it's the perfect texture, has so much flavor, and you can tell it's homemade. (Saving my mango margarita for later! So good!) I should have taken pics of everything, because the food LOOKS good but tastes even better.</Review>

<username>Bryan Bishop</username>< Review>
Nice to be out and sit down to have dinner. We opted for the patio even though inside dining was available. Decent food but subpar service. We waited forever to order and when asking for extra napkins we never got any and salsa took two times to ask and then we had a bunch of salsa and no chips until our entrees arrived. Decent taco and enchilada but the Chile relleno was really disappointing. Good margaritas and friendly service but overall not as good as our normal spot "Mucho Mas" which we hope comes back by next year at the latest. In the meantime this will do for now unless I find something better. Just thankful to be out and about again!</Review>
